  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_84ee85c5-f243-4453-b02b-d682e2b8eebd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer5494879451282520528">Deacon has an ugly history, a history that broke him, leaving him a ghost of a man. Out of necessity, he left the normal world to descend into the criminal world and found he fit. So he stayed. Cold as ice and living off the grid, Deacon has no intention to connect, not with anyone.<br/><br/>Then he returns to some remote cabins in the Colorado Mountains and finds they have new owne</span>
  <span id="freeText5494879451282520528" style="display:none">Deacon has an ugly history, a history that broke him, leaving him a ghost of a man. Out of necessity, he left the normal world to descend into the criminal world and found he fit. So he stayed. Cold as ice and living off the grid, Deacon has no intention to connect, not with anyone.<br /><br />Then he returns to some remote cabins in the Colorado Mountains and finds they have new owners. One of them is Cassidy Swallow, a young woman willing to work hard to live her quiet dream in a house by a river surrounded by aspen and pine.<br /><br />Suddenly, Deacon finds he’s at war. Cassidy’s pull for him to connect is strong. He fights it, but he loses, always coming back for more. But when he does, he gives her nothing.<br /><br />From the first time she sees him, Cassidy knows Deacon is dead inside. She knows he’s the kind of man who could destroy a woman. But one night when Deacon’s control slips, Cassidy takes a chance.<br /><br />He might break her. He also might be her dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5494879451282520528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/756132958" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/756132958?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=author-kristen-ashley">author-kristen-ashley</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756132958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2725059528047034412">Re-read 12/17/14...The review below still stands...<br/><br/><b>2.5-3 Stars of Disappointment</b><br/><br/>It <b>kills</b> me to rate another KA so low, but that's just how I feel about this book. <br/><br/>I'm going to keep this short...just because. <br/><br/>It started off really strong and I was loving it.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411577295ra/11251014.gif' width='455' height='307' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I just knew <i>Deacon</i> was destined for greatness. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411577295i/11251015.jpg' width='500' height='281' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Until it wasn't.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411577295ra/11251016.gif' width='500' height='279' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The ENTIRE book was about Deacon and Cassidy and their relationship. <br/><br/>No Rock Chick-esque crime/shenanigan aspects. <br/>No Reese or Finn-esque side characters. <br/>Nothing ELSE.<br/><br/>Which would</span>
  <span id="freeText2725059528047034412" style="display:none">Re-read 12/17/14...The review below still stands...<br><br><b>2.5-3 Stars of Disappointment</b><br><br>It <b>kills</b> me to rate another KA so low, but that's just how I feel about this book. <br><br>I'm going to keep this short...just because. <br><br>It started off really strong and I was loving it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411577295ra/11251014.gif" width="455" height="307" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just knew <i>Deacon</i> was destined for greatness. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411577295i/11251015.jpg" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Until it wasn't.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411577295ra/11251016.gif" width="500" height="279" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The ENTIRE book was about Deacon and Cassidy and their relationship. <br><br>No Rock Chick-esque crime/shenanigan aspects. <br>No Reese or Finn-esque side characters. <br>Nothing ELSE.<br><br>Which would have been totally fine...except that it started to get really slow and kind of redundant. <br><br>Also - in the beginning of the book, there is a "disclaimer" regarding some bdsm/butt play shenanigans that were going to be afoot - and I was like YES! <br><br>Bring. It. On. <br><br>Well, it got brought on. And it was...Okay. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411578087ra/11251095.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Until it wasn't. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411578087i/11251096.jpg" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm sorry, but a supposed <i>"Badass"</i> (a word that was soooooo overused in this book, it's ridiculous) like Deacon? I just don't see him allowing ANYONE to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[shove a butt plug up his ass. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411578349i/11251134.jpg" width="480" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>There are other ways to prove trust, people!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The words "Badass" and "Beauty" need to get shoved up someone's ass though, I tell you what.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And when Cassidy finds out (or thinks she finds out) about Deacon's secret, she sends him off with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ an overplayed Christina Aguilera song??? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> REALLY? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411579029i/11251260.jpg" width="500" height="394" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't know. <br><br>It started off so strong and I was so excited about it. But, at the end of the day...I just thought the story got boring (by 80% I was almost skimming...skimming a KA!!!), there wasn't enough <i>real</i> communication between the characters when there needed to be most (instead we got <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[butt plug-gate <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>), and overall this just fell flat for me. <br><br>All I know is, a book that I have been anticipating for EVER (and probably the most that I can remember in recent years) is the final of the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/81946-the-three" rel="nofollow noopener">Three Series</a>. <br><br>So even though this one missed the mark for me, I have my fingers crossed for that one. <br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br>Please be good, please be good, please be good...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410353792ra/11096248.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_714944310" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/714944310" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/714944310?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer714944310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10089502191900661664"><b>5 Bossy Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/35933505-1ee9-4196-9866-890a85863d36_zps82b15bc6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308830.jpg' alt=' photo 35933505-1ee9-4196-9866-890a85863d36_zps82b15bc6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Kristen Ashely’s Unfinished Heroes series is my favorite of hers. Not only do we have Knight- aka the Daddy- aka Christy’s book husband, but we have Creed and Raid which are pretty great as well. When I heard Deacon was getting a book, I was pretty freaking excited. I had very high expectations for this book, and I wasn’t let down. Knight is still my favorite of the series, but this was a close second! <i>Deacon</i> is not only insanely hot, but we have a sexy alpha antihero, a kick a</span>
  <span id="freeText10089502191900661664" style="display:none"><b>5 Bossy Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/35933505-1ee9-4196-9866-890a85863d36_zps82b15bc6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308830.jpg" alt=" photo 35933505-1ee9-4196-9866-890a85863d36_zps82b15bc6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kristen Ashely’s Unfinished Heroes series is my favorite of hers. Not only do we have Knight- aka the Daddy- aka Christy’s book husband, but we have Creed and Raid which are pretty great as well. When I heard Deacon was getting a book, I was pretty freaking excited. I had very high expectations for this book, and I wasn’t let down. Knight is still my favorite of the series, but this was a close second! <i>Deacon</i> is not only insanely hot, but we have a sexy alpha antihero, a kick ass hilariously fun heroine, and a great story. You can’t ask for more that that!<br><br>Cassidy is living her dream, doing what she’s always wanted to do... but is she really living? She has always wanted to live in the Colorado Mountains. She’s now the proud owner of Glacier Lily Cottages. She rents out 11 different cabins by the night. She didn’t plan on doing this alone. She planned on doing it with her man, but that didn’t quite pan out. She’s happy where she is, and she’s happy with her work... but still, something is missing. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/60888c20-9d47-47b2-a5df-db4664281273_zps5a67e15b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308831.jpg" alt=" photo 60888c20-9d47-47b2-a5df-db4664281273_zps5a67e15b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Since the very start of her running this business, Cassidy has a man, a costumer that visits cabin 11 frequently. He says his name is John Priest. He’s tall, dark, handsome, and a little bit scary. He’s also quiet, brooding and rugged. For years he comes by. Sometimes every few weeks, sometimes every few months, but he always shows. And she always keeps cabin 11 open for him if she can. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/353e7854-0019-4ecd-857f-284ca81ad312_zpsb2044070.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308832.jpg" alt=" photo 353e7854-0019-4ecd-857f-284ca81ad312_zpsb2044070.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Deacon has a mysterious past. We’re not sure who he really is, what he does for a living or any of that. What he does isn’t exactly on the radar, or even legal for that matter. Something happened to him to make him so closed off. He has very few people in his life he trusts, or who know the real him. He has no real home. But for some reason, or because of one particular woman, he is constantly drawn back to Glacier Lily Cottages when he’s not working. <br><br>It’s obvious Cassidy and Deacon are drawn to each other. For years they fight that pull. Deacon knows he wouldn’t be good for a woman like her. And Cassidy knows Deacon has a dangerous side. But they can only fight their feelings for so long... Until it all comes out in the open. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Not easy, fightin’ your pull. Wantin’ to be right here. Knowin’ I was no good for you. Prayin’ you’d get a man so when I’d come back I’d have a reason to stay away.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/71e4f03c-7127-467a-85a5-26f2f2327638_zpsd3d1ccf7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308833.jpg" alt=" photo 71e4f03c-7127-467a-85a5-26f2f2327638_zpsd3d1ccf7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You’re the most beautiful woman I’ve seen in my entire fuckin’ life.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Their relationship had a unique start. It definitely wasn’t insta-love, it was more like a slow build up. They weren’t able to spend all kinds of time together, but anytime Deacon wasn’t working, he was with Cassidy. It was the only place he actually wanted to be. He hadn’t had a home in a very long time, but with Cassidy, he was finding one again. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/fbe13a60-1448-4c43-b222-4f45b9c71e78_zpsbec7b67f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308834.jpg" alt=" photo fbe13a60-1448-4c43-b222-4f45b9c71e78_zpsbec7b67f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cassidy was an incredible heroine. One of my favorite KA heroines for sure. I can’t think of one time she was unlikable or annoying. She worked hard, she was sweet, funny, stubborn, bossy and spunky. I loved her attitude. So many scenes with her had me laughing out loud. Because come on- how true is this statement? <br><i>
  <blockquote>“ I don’t watch the news, Deacon. It’s televised depression.”</blockquote>
</i><br> Talking to herself in the hardware store... then the grocery store... I can’t even tell you how many times I’ve done that! I love that she speaks her mind and is outgoing and strong. You have to have that backbone when your with a badass alpha. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Total boss.” <br>“A girl has to be when her man’s a bad ass.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And that’s exactly what Deacon was. A bad ass alpha. He seemed like this complete hard ass, stoic and uncaring at the beginning, but that’s not him at all. Deacon is a caring and protective man. He’s just had a past that has made him a bit damaged. Then there is Deacon in the bedroom... this book may be Kristen’s hottest book yet. Seriously scorching hot and kinky. I loved it! Deacon was a bossy in the bedroom, but let himself be vulnerable too. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/abc6f83e-fc10-4b2c-b495-fe907985db13_zpsb701ed24.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308835.jpg" alt=" photo abc6f83e-fc10-4b2c-b495-fe907985db13_zpsb701ed24.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Deacon and Cassidy didn’t have the easiest relationship, but they both wanted it, wanted each other. <i>Deacon</i> is not only a beautiful romance, but also an emotional tale of a man getting over his past and a woman helping him learn to love and trust again. <br><br>  I love the way Kristen Ashley writes. I love her details, her story telling ability, and her fantastic heroines and hot as hell alphas. When I read books like this, I remember why she is my favorite author. After reading <i>Deacon</i>, I was a 100% happy and satisfied reader, and there is no better feeling than that!<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“No boundaries. That’s us, Cassidy. That’s who we are. That’s what we were both searchin’ for.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/f3b3d542-1ed3-42a1-8b37-2b3ca78121a6_zps10c5ecd2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411991135i/11308836.jpg" alt=" photo f3b3d542-1ed3-42a1-8b37-2b3ca78121a6_zps10c5ecd2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10089502191900661664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1012214138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11519110488192984141"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 STARS :::</b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411679571i/11264478.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> My casting for Deacon.... ;) </i><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411593491i/11253267._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Kristen Ashley does it again!! And now we have a new badass Alpha male hero to swoon over :D</b><br/><br/>Meet Deacon: Tall. Dark. Rugged. Cold on the outside. Closed off from the world. Cassidy could tell with one look that this man was alive on the outside, but dead on the inside. And she wasn't wrong.<br/><br/>Her whole life, she dreamed of owning cabins in the mountains and living a life there. And, being the can-do type of woman that she was</span>
  <span id="freeText11519110488192984141" style="display:none"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 STARS :::</b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411679571i/11264478.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> My casting for Deacon.... ;) </i><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411593491i/11253267._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kristen Ashley does it again!! And now we have a new badass Alpha male hero to swoon over :D</b><br><br>Meet Deacon: Tall. Dark. Rugged. Cold on the outside. Closed off from the world. Cassidy could tell with one look that this man was alive on the outside, but dead on the inside. And she wasn't wrong.<br><br>Her whole life, she dreamed of owning cabins in the mountains and living a life there. And, being the can-do type of woman that she was, she did just that. She followed her dreams and made them her reality.<br><br>This was where Deacon entered her life. He came every few months and rented cabin eleven. Each time it was the same: cash, few words, nothing else, and then he was gone again. Outwardly he showed no sign of either caring for her as a person or noticing her as a woman except for a few fleeting moments when something slipped and she knews that somewhere deep down he cared, even if he hid it from the world.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"He scared the heck out of me. But this was only part of the reason he scared the heck out of me. The other part, the bigger part, was even feeling all that, I had a nearly-overwhelming urge to go to him and wrap my arms around him. Tight. And maybe never let go. For eternity."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>So their relationship grew over the years. It was a slow burn and a beautiful build up. No insta-love, but rather a genuinely believable progression. His job took him away frequently for weeks or months at a time... and even though it seemed that he wanted nothing to do with her, the more they got to know each other, the more it became clear just how much this badass man really cared for her.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"I'm away, Cassie, do not ever doubt this is precisely where I'd rather be."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Cassidy was an absolutely amazing, strong woman and one of the best heroines KA has written. Oh my gosh, this girl was AWESOME!!! She was in charge of her life, earning her way, following her dreams and her heart, and making something beautiful out of it.<br><br>I loved the way she saw right through Deacon's cold, distant, aloof, badass exterior and wasn't intimidated by him. It's like she instinctively knew he was a good man no matter how dangerous he seemed. It really warms my heart seeing such strong heroines who aren't afraid to go toe-to-toe with the Alphas!!<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"So he was scary. So he was badass. So he was closed off in a way that he'd made clear more than once he was never going to open.<br>I didn't care.<br>I had this one shot, the only one I knew I'd ever get, so I was going to take it."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Beneath his stone cold exterior, Deacon was a wonderful hero. Such a good guy. He was really deep, respectful, kind, caring, protective... and everything you can imagine from a genuinely good person. He lived in a dangerous world but it didn't define him. His actions defined him and that was enough for me.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Not easy, fightin' your pull. Wantin' to be right here. Knowin' I was no good for you. Prayin' you'd get a man so when I'd come back I'd have a reason to stay away."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Cassie's on-going list of badass do's and don'ts throughout the book were too funny!! Not to mention the Badass Zones and Badass Boundaries... all of these kept a big smile on my face for pages on end.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Don't be playful when I'm feeling emotional."<br>"You get I'm a badass."<br>"Hard to miss, Deacon."<br>"Then don't tell me when to be playful. Badassess don't like that shit."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I loved their dynamic and the way they always worked towards trying to find a balance between finding equality in the relationship while still respecting each other. He let her be who she was but was always there to have her back and support her without being over bearing. Deacon had somehow found the perfect Alpha balance. And in turn, her strength and kind heart was his perfect match.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>He glowered at me.<br>Then he grinned.<br>"Total boss."<br>"A girl has to be when her man's a badass."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Not to mention that this is definitely one of KA's hottest books. There's all manner of kinky bondage in it (but you'll have to be patient, cuz it's in the second half. First comes the relationship development, then comes the kink). But yeah, I was definitely fanning myself!! Hot, hot, hotttttt!!! <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Love is trust, Cassie, you taught me that."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Overall, this is a quiet book. Don't expect edge-of-your-seat drama that's not what this book is about. It's a love story. It's a romance. Just a damaged badass and a big-hearted gal falling in love in the Mountains. Both Cassie and Deacon were really sensible people. Him with a lot of damage and emotional scarring from his past. Her with a big enough heart to just love him for who he was. I loved the way they completed each other. And I loved watching their relationship grow and develop with every new page. As I said, it's a slow burn. But it was realistically paced. Totally awesome. Oh, and kinky too. Don't forget the bondage ;)<br><br>There are many different kinds of Alphas and, as long as they have respect for their women, I love them all. But I feel like I had an extra understanding for Deacon. Everything about him made sense. He had no real "Omg-I-Can't-Believe-He-Just-Said-That" moments. Even when he did do shocking things, I just felt, as Cassie did, I felt that there was a reason for his actions. And they usually made sense. He was fair, kind, and caring. The closed-off, secret side of him was understandable. And even when he was distant, I felt like I trusted that there was a good reason for it. He just didn't seem like the kind of guy who would be that way without one. And, as it was later revealed, he did indeed have a good reason. I guess... I just trusted him.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Anything. You want it, I got it in me to give it to you, you got anything from me.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>In the interest of full honesty, I'll say there were four small things that I had issue with in this book, so it wasn't fully perfect. But none of them were anything big enough to cause me to dislike the book and none of them bad enough for me to go into long detail either. But I'm just telling you that they're there.<br><br>Kristen Ashley is so gifted at getting you right inside her characters heads to the point where you feel completely in sync with their thoughts. And the language she writes in is downright awesome. Yes, its english, but it's almost as if she has her very own "badass dialect" that is entirely unique to her. There's Alpha speak, but then there's KA Alpha speak and I absolutely LOVE IT!!!<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"If we have daughters I'm starting How to Deal with Badasses when they're five."<br><br>His eyes were lit but his expression was full-on tender when he returned, "We have boys, they get How to Deal with Stubborn Bitches Who Argue About Meaningless Shit starting at three."<br><br>"Again, women dislike being called bitches," I shot back.<br><br>"That'll be part of my lesson to the boys."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Finally, just because I'm being asked this a lot... You can read this as a standalone if you want, but there are cameos from the other guys in the series towards the end of the book. Knowing their stories isn't vital to understanding this one, but being emotionally attached to them might be (otherwise they're just a bunch of Deacon's friends who show up). So it's really up to you. But it can be read alone.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Heart and soul, gut and balls, I love you. There’s no one I’d rather hold. Not until I’m eighty. Not until the day I die.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><b>Rating: 4.5 stars. Contemporary Adult Romance.</b><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062552855" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11265829386209263707"><br/><br/>This was “typical” KA. Has the term “KA” been added to any official dictionary yet? It should be! Halfway through I was wanting something more to happen. I think I had a hankering for the exciting stuff that happened in the Colorado series. I read one review that said it was a “slow burn” (Jennifer, I think) and yes, it was. But when we got to about 80% it all sort of took off and we got to know more about Deacon and why he was the way he was.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>… dead man walking …</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261981._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yes, I love all the flowery, </span>
  <span id="freeText11265829386209263707" style="display:none"><br><br>This was “typical” KA. Has the term “KA” been added to any official dictionary yet? It should be! Halfway through I was wanting something more to happen. I think I had a hankering for the exciting stuff that happened in the Colorado series. I read one review that said it was a “slow burn” (Jennifer, I think) and yes, it was. But when we got to about 80% it all sort of took off and we got to know more about Deacon and why he was the way he was.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>… dead man walking …</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261981._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, I love all the flowery, descriptions that come with a KA book. Descriptions of the clothes, the interiors, the sinks even.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658555i/11262023._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The sex is HOT.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261979._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Badasses know what they want, definitely know what they need, and don’t settle for anything less.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394034528i/8798779.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Loved that we got to meet characters from previous books.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“It was my turn to let my eyes travel over his features. Take in his male beauty. Memorize it. Do it knowing that as crazy as it sounded, I’d never forget him. For reasons I didn’t know and would never have the opportunity to understand, there would always be a part of me that would long for him. There would always be thoughts in the back of my mind plaguing me, haunting me, making me wonder, if he let me in, even just a little, how it could have been. I stopped thinking these thoughts when the pad of his thumb whispered across my lips. That was when the tears pricked my eyes. Because I knew that was when he was going to let me go. For always.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261980._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The story focuses on their relationship. On how Deacon wants to be the man for Cassie but is convinced that he can not be.<br><br>He is an ass at times. But he does redeem himself. Aw, I loved him.<br><br>I found her to be a very strong character. She took no shit from him. She was independent, ran her own business.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658264i/11261997._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Strange how life connected like that ...</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I know some reviews hinted that Deacon was not really an “anti-hero” like Knight maybe. TBH, I have read the other books but cannot really remember them. Need to do a re-read maybe.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261984._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Any author that incorporates music and lyrics into a book is usually a winner for me. I am a Rock Chick at heart. Eventhough I have not read that series. BTW, Happy Birthday <i>The Boss</i> – yesterday he turned 65!! Looking good, old man!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261985._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, I got my epilogue but it was more of a prologue for the next book (well, I thought so).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261986.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>KA is an auto-buy for me. One or two of her books I have been a bit disappointed in. But, overall, this author can do no wrong.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411658041i/11261987._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_1062316882" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062316882" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062316882?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22846841-deacon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=author-kristen-ashley">author-kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062316882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6272609086861670353"><br/><b>
  <i>"It's a beautiful war, baby." <br/>He dipped so close, the tips of our noses <br/>brushed but his eyes never left mine. <br/>"And I...just won."</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span> <br/><br/>Deacon and Cassidy’s story was a slow burn tale of a mysterious hot guy named John Priest renting the now infamous cabin number 11 sporadically for several years. <br/><br/>One night their dynamics changes and the couple is left with the question of where do they go from here? <br/> <br/><b>
  <i>”After last night, we changed,” he responded immediately. “And that change can go</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText6272609086861670353" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>"It's a beautiful war, baby." <br>He dipped so close, the tips of our noses <br>brushed but his eyes never left mine. <br>"And I...just won."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>Deacon and Cassidy’s story was a slow burn tale of a mysterious hot guy named John Priest renting the now infamous cabin number 11 sporadically for several years. <br><br>One night their dynamics changes and the couple is left with the question of where do they go from here? <br> <br><b>
  <i>”After last night, we changed,” he responded immediately. “And that change can go two ways. Either I drive away and we never see each other again or I don’t and we find out what that change is gonna mean. Read down to your bones, woman, and do it now. Which way do you want that change to be?”</i>
</b><br><br>Cassidy was one kick ass lead and Deacon he was the complete broken alpha package. Cassidy goes for it but who is John Priest/Deacon? He is a mystery that he doesn’t plan on explaining. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’m away, Cassie do not ever doubt this is precisely where I’d rather be.”</i>
</b><br><br>The sex scenes were on fire and the Queen actually gives a reader a warning and boy did she deliver... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411568443i/11249615._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Doubts and questions that Deacon won’t answer breaks these two apart. Deach is left struggling with the man he used to be and the man he has become.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Tried to be dead again when I left you, Cassie. Dead doesn’t hurt. Tried fuckin’ hard to find it. But I couldn’t find it. You lived in me.”</i>
</b><br><br>There were also cameos of all of my favorite guys from previous books in the series and the tie-ins to those books totally wowed me. I loved the progression of the resort as well as the delivery of who Deacon is, what has broken him and my darn Kindle was smoking when Deacon gives himself to Cassidy. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br> <br>Overall, the setting was gorgeous I would definitely book a stay if Cassidy would start providing the towels. I loved everything about this book totally K.A. magic for me!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411591682i/11253037._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_745508624" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/745508624" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/745508624?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<div id="review_1063128658" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1063128658" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1063128658?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1063128658" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5308644898789817266"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br/><br/>Don't be fooled by my rating because I actually enjoyed this book. It was shorter than most KA book which I didn't mind. It was also hot, which was a plus. But...there are a few things that bothered me. Let's get to the positives first. <br/><br/>1. Deacon. I am probably one of the few who didn't mind that Deacon was a watered down version of previous KA alphas especially in this series. We all know what this series is about. The male leads in this series have typically been edgier and darker co</span>
  <span id="freeText5308644898789817266" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br /><br />Don't be fooled by my rating because I actually enjoyed this book. It was shorter than most KA book which I didn't mind. It was also hot, which was a plus. But...there are a few things that bothered me. Let's get to the positives first. <br /><br />1. Deacon. I am probably one of the few who didn't mind that Deacon was a watered down version of previous KA alphas especially in this series. We all know what this series is about. The male leads in this series have typically been edgier and darker compared to KA's other series. That said, Deacon was pretty tame in the bossy alpha department. I didn't mind this at all. He had a lot of vulnerabilities for a KA hero, which I really liked. <br /><br />2. The length. KA made the length work. There were no unnecessary descriptions of clothing, decor or anything. <br /><br />3. Cassidy. I liked her. She was steady throughout the book. <br /><br />4. The sex was hot. For sure. Deacon and Cassidy have awesome chemistry which I really liked. <br /><br />Now, what I didn't like or wasn't too crazy about.<br /><br />1. The over use of the words like beauty and badass. KA needs to retire beauty. I still can't imagine some badass saying that to a girl while he's banging her. <br /><br />And a badass wouldn't say badass unless badass is a girl and likes to wear to pink. I don't know. Is there like a rule or something that part of being a badass is not saying the word badass or even acknowledge being one?? Lol! I just found that trite and cringe-worthy.<br /><br />2. Again with the whole renovation thing. <i>Sigh</i> I had Kaleidoscope flashbacks with that one. <br /><br />3. The general lack of grittiness that I associated with this series. Don't get me wrong, I liked that this book was relationship-focused but it felt like we only get to see half of Deacon. I missed seeing the other side of him, that part which made him such an asset to Knight &amp; Co. We didn't get to see that here.<br /><br />As a bonus, I'm also gonna list the things that had me going "Huh" or just generally left me "Meh".<br /><br />1. The kink. What separates the Unfinished Hero Series from KA's other series was the kink. But frankly, I just generally found them awkward. Not because I don't like them in my books -- God knows I've enjoyed far kinkier books in the past -- but I don't think KA has managed to find her kinky voice yet. It's all very mechanical to me. I found their vanilla sex better. <br /><br />2. The pacing. Yeah, which sounds contradictory because I liked the length. It wasn't bad but it wasn't great either because there were too many lulls and not too many excitement. It worked in the whole scheme of the book but I wish there could have been more excitement, I guess.<br /><br />3. The use of songs. Sometimes they work sometimes they don't. Sometimes I just don't care either way. Don't get me wrong I liked the songs KA chose. The messages of the songs fit those moments between Cassie and Deacon. What I wasn't really sure about was the way the two went about it, you know. I'm like, "What are you 15?" I mean, seriously? I kinda expected Deacon to make a mix tape for Cassie to express his feels. Again, nothing wrong with that but Deacon? I mean, maybe a 15 year old Deacon but a 38 year old Deacon? Hmmm...Not gonna lie, I loved Beautiful War but it just...I dunno. It was cute and all but I'm not sure if that was consistent with the characters at all. <br /><br />Overall, still an enjoyable read. Better than the Promise for sure. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5308644898789817266" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/732082666" />
    <a title="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks"><img alt="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599759753p2/18387313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/732082666?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳" href="/user/show/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks">Ⓐlleskelle - teamSøren♗ ⊲I like big b00ks⊳</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22846841-deacon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=contemp">contemp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=dirty-talker">dirty-talker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=00-on-my-ipad">00-on-my-ipad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=angst-o-fest">angst-o-fest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=neighbor-to-lovers">neighbor-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer732082666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2658323057952750597"><br/>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<b> 5 STARS </b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/><br/><i>Friends, I’m a Kristen Ashley fan, but I’m also first and foremost a woman who speaks her own mind. Therefore the following review isn’t just me gushing over another KA book. If I were to fangirl, I’d simply tell you to read everything KA wrote, that I enjoyed all her books, (Okay, you got me here, I DID) and that there’s no reason you wouldn’t too!<br/>No, this review will be about sharing feelings being delivered to me straight to the heart, without any warning. I need </i></span>
  <span id="freeText2658323057952750597" style="display:none"><br>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<b> 5 STARS </b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><br><i>Friends, I’m a Kristen Ashley fan, but I’m also first and foremost a woman who speaks her own mind. Therefore the following review isn’t just me gushing over another KA book. If I were to fangirl, I’d simply tell you to read everything KA wrote, that I enjoyed all her books, (Okay, you got me here, I DID) and that there’s no reason you wouldn’t too!<br>No, this review will be about sharing feelings being delivered to me straight to the heart, without any warning. I need to let it out!</i><br>(And a warning, you may be on your way to the longest review, ever, so bear with me!)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253996._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Dream come true, seated deep inside you in this bed.<br>Six years, laid in this bed, you up at the house, wantin’ this.<br>Dream come true.”</blockquote>
</b><br>I did not expect the level of emotions I felt reading Deacon and Cassie’ story. I thought I’d signed —wrongly— for a gritty and action packed adventure, cleverly entwined with romance, a dark and broken man and woman finding their reason to be, as it was the case in this series’ previous books. I couldn’t have been more wrong. This book was so much more than the usual action/love story. I didn’t even check the blurb before diving in, I figured it was unnecessary as I loved all the previous Unfinished Heroes, and I’m glad I did so, the surprise was all the more welcomed!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411783614i/11274070._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411783614i/11274071._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Deacon</b> is the fourth book in Kristen Ashley’s <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/77851-unfinished-hero" rel="nofollow noopener">Unfinished Heroes series</a>
</b>. We met Deacon briefly in Raid’s book, maybe even Creed…? Damn memory, I guess this calls for a re-read of this series soon! All I remembered was him being kind of a lone wolf.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253992._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cassidy Swallow is an ambitious, self made woman, with her dream all laid out for her, she left her home in Oklahoma with her eyes set on her dream since she’s a teenager. Living her life in the beauty that are Colorado mountains, owning her own business, and enjoying a peaceful and happy life with the man of her heart, Grant. <i>(Come on, she is not the only woman whose dream is going to live in Colorado. That’s where all the Alpha badasses are. Keep a cabin open for me, Cassie!)</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273133._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253987._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779664ra/11273351.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, as we enter this story today, Cassidy is 24, and she is just setting up her Rental Cabins business with her boyfriend, Grant. Everything is going according to plan, well, for Cassidy at least.<br>Grant is just not settling to the business owner’s life, having to prioritize work over play time doesn’t work for him.<br><br>Cassidy is becoming more and more conscious of Grant’s moody temper and non support. She doesn’t recognize the man she fell in love back in Oklahoma, <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273135._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enters the picture a man, a customer more precisely, interrupting yet another argument between Grant and Cassidy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253990._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Tall. Dark-haired. Rugged-featured. His large frame built tough and solid.<br>…he was terrifying.<br>Utterly.<br>Huge. Dark. His face a cold, emotionlessness mask.<br>He existed.<br>He did not live. He did not feel. He did not smile. He did not laugh.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Ladies, meet John Priest : <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411429925i/11226588._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779664ra/11273352.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779664ra/11273353.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Cassidy and Grant’s relationship is slowly sinking down the drain, we are spectators to Cassidy slow and steady life as the owner of <b>Glacier Lily Cottages,</b> with glimpses of this mysterious John Priest (our Deacon), returning customer, who continues year after year to rent his secluded <b>cabin 11</b>.<br><br>From the moment she laid eyes on him, Cassidy felt an irresistible pull toward her most mysterious customer. <br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“The other part, the bigger part, was even feeling all that, I had a near-overwhelming urge to go to him and wrap my arms around him.<br>Tight.<br>And maybe never let go.<br>For eternity.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411787518i/11275032._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know. Insta lust. Love. But not quite. And you know what? I don’t care, she wasn’t declaring her love and having his babies right this minute. She just knew this was the kind of man whom if he decided to give himself, would be a dream of a man. <br>For years, their relation will stay purely professional, observing a gradual yearning, wanting, and I loved every aspect of this scarcely slow burn.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779664ra/11273354.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Deacon’s not a man she could easily covet anyway, he is closed off, cold, distant and shares only the utter minimum. He doesn’t talk. He mutters. He growls. His words are clipped. And he made sure to give her NO reason to get attached, he made sure to keep her <i>safe</i>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253993._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Until one night, everything is going to <i>finally</i> change, an unfortunate accident in her establishment is forcing Deacon to stay close to Cassie. To show her <b>he cares</b>. That he cared for <i>years</i>.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Every time I show, I pray to God there’ll be another truck outside your house, a man in your bed. Every time I show, nothin’. You’re alone. No fuckin’ clue why. You the way you are. Goofy. Sweet. Hard-workin’. Happy to sit outside on a porch and sit quiet, doin’ nothin’ but bein’ and listenin’ to a river rush by. The way you look. No man?<br>It makes no fuckin’ sense. Then you rent a cabin to me knowin’ you should show me the road and that makes even less sense.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411784654ra/11274371.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779120ra/11273139.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779120ra/11273140.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once again, Kristen Ashley provided steam in spades! From the moment Deacon and Cassie "change", the level of hotness is hitting high, the chemistry between them is explosive, rendering carnal their every touch. The sex scenes that are offered here… I have no words.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411785003ra/11274410.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411601395i/11254119._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411783614ra/11274072.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411782741ra/11273905.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cassidy has an unfulfilled curiosity regarding bondage, and well, Deacon being a man of many talents, demonstrates his skills, and be prepared : Deacon vanilla style is hot, but throw in a little kink and it becomes sizzling hot!!! I saw an update here 2 days ago : "HOSE ME DOWN" <i>(Maura, was it you?)</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411783614ra/11274073.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411782741i/11273906._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411782741i/11273907._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>KA accomplished to enhance my pleasure reading this book even more, by giving me <b>A DIRTY TALKER</b>!!!<br>I loved Creed for that, but seriously Deacon plays in his own league. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411782741i/11273908._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779120ra/11273141.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Baby, that pussy on my mouth, your ass in my hands, the noises you make fillin’ the room, knowin’ I get to drive deep in your wet, tight cunt while you’re still moanin’ for me. Then after I give it to you, and you give it to me, I get to bed down with you tucked tight. You don’t think that makes me happy, you’re fuckin’ crazy.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“I didn’t just ride you until your pussy exploded. You did that to my dick. Fuck, watchin’ all that beauty go wild, takin’ my cock, enough to undo a man. Add that cunt so wet and tight…Jesus.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Somehow along the way, Cassidy is breaking this ruthless man’s walls.<br>With her kindness, her smartass-ness, her Christmas kisses, her eyes and all the little things that makes Cassie who she is. She is giving him a real shot at something genuine, a good life, with an honest and hard working woman.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273540._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779120ra/11273142.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253991._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But Deacon being a shell of a man, a broken man, a man whose dreams have been ripped apart… Well this man is not ready to give it all to Cassie yet. Something’s still having a hold on him, and we can just hope for Deacon to work his shit out. For Cassie’s sake.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Say something,” I begged on a whisper.<br>He said nothing.<br>“Say something,” I repeated, my eyes burning now for a different reason, tears fighting to be unleashed.”<br>“You need to say something, Deacon. You need to give me something, anything.”<br>He didn’t speak.<br>“You said you’d give me anything,” I accused.<br>“Say something,” I snapped. “You have to. You don’t get that, Deacon.” I jabbed a finger to the picture on the floor. “You don’t get that from me. You don’t bring that in my house. To my cabins. To my bed.” I sucked in breath and screeched, “Say something!” </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273541._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is slow paced, so very so. At one point I felt like this was going nowhere to be honest, I was pondering what was so awesome about this rugged man being domesticated… Still enjoying the characteristic KA touch, but wondering when this "Unfinished Hero" business was going to burst in. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273542._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273543._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I should have known something was building, something I wasn’t aware of, something beautiful, but before getting "it", I had to know who was behind "Deacon Deacon". <br>Trust me when I say that Deacon was as "Unfinished" as the others, Knight, Raid, Creed… <br>From this moment on, with all the music references, knowing all too well the songs KA referred to… It gave me the chills. This gave a whole new meaning to the story. All the little moment and the descriptiveness KA is well known for… Those moments were golden. Even more so after reading the book. I spent 2 days thinking about it all, I’m currently writing this review, listening to Kings of Leon’s Beautiful War. <br>Make yourself a favor, and when mentioned in the book, play the songs, it’ll enhance the experience, feels, tears guaranteed! <i>
  <a href="http://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLSuBSDgWZMVwSTg-SxmwER_wlSraV7aAo" rel="nofollow noopener">(Playlist Youtube : clic)</a>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273544._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273545._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Want ’em, woman. Two, definitely, maybe three.”<br>Oh yes.<br>Gleefully happy.<br>“Yeah?” I whispered.<br>“Yeah,” he whispered back.<br>“I want two, maybe three, too.”<br>His eyes lit and he pressed closer. “Miracle.”<br>That confused me.<br>“Sorry?”<br>“Somethin’ my Cassie Boss isn’t gonna fight about.”</blockquote>
</b><br>I loved Cassidy, she was smart, sassy, always a retort on the tip of her tongue, that made her a really top of the class KA heroine! I loved her cataloguing of every Badass Behavior, she was hilarious. Witty and sweet, caring and loving. Everything Deacon’s needed to heal.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Not stupid enough to know I’d win every fight, but you taught me I could take care of a woman again. You taught me I could be trusted with her. You taught me I could make her laugh and smile and you gave me back what it feels like, doin’ that for a woman you love.<br>…You taught me a lot of things, Cassidy.”</blockquote>
</b><br>The banter in this book was to die for!!! Kristen Ashley delivered banter at its finest! And it was all the more hilarious to witness this cold man goofing around with Cassie.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411780417i/11273546._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Those two, three babies?”<br>My body tensed. “Yeah?”<br>“This stays good, woman, wanna make ’em with you.”<br>I closed my eyes tight.<br>“I know that’s too soon. I also don’t give a fuck,” he continued.<br>“It is not too soon,” I replied firmly.<br>“Fuck, my Cassie.”<br>“That’s me, your Cassie. And you’re my Deacon.”<br>His hand started sliding up my side as his lips ordered, “Quiet.”<br>“You should know, I’m claiming you.”<br>“Woman, quiet,” he growled.<br>“Too much too soon?” I asked, like it was a dare.<br>“Fuck no.”<br>“Okay, then quit your bitching.”<br>He glowered at me. Then he grinned.<br>“Total boss.”<br>“A girl has to be when her man’s a badass.”<br>“Like you weren’t one before.”<br>“Whatever.”<br>“She was one before,” he muttered.<br><br><blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Jesus, you’re so much of a woman, you’re more woman than any woman I’ve met.”<br>I started getting peeved again.<br>“You say that like it’s bad,” I replied sharply.<br>“Hang on, Cassidy, I’m still adjusting to your last mood swing.”<br>I glared at him and saw the crinkles by his eyes.<br>He was teasing.<br>“Don’t be playful when I’m feeling emotional,” I ordered.<br>To this, he strangely replied, “You get I’m a badass.”<br>“Hard to miss, Deacon,” I returned.<br>“Then don’t tell me when to be playful. Badasses don’t like that shit.”</blockquote>
</blockquote>
</b><br>As much as he was dark and aloof, Deacon was sweet! The things he said to Cassie throughout the book… Lovely things, I was literally swooning every time. For a man who cut ties, a man supposedly rusty, he was at the top of his game!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411779120ra/11273143.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411784654ra/11274372.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411779120i/11273132.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">“Woman, if you don’t already know that you’ve been on my mind every day for the last six years, I got no clue how to communicate that to you. Now that I’ve had you, that shit has not changed. It’s just got worse. Now it’s not every day. It’s every hour. I don’t fight it, every minute. Fuck, every second, I don’t keep it in check. Every second, I’m thinkin’ of you, thinkin’ of gettin’ shit done, but only so I can get back to you.”</blockquote>
</b><br>The book already won me over, but it was without counting the cameos! Raid, Knight, Creed, Marcus and their woman are making appearances, even Maxwell and Nina are mentioned. I loved it! Kristen Ashley weaved in the Colorado series, the Rock Chick series, The Unfinished Heroes series all in one book! <br><b>Deacon</b> was definitely not built the same as the previous books in this series, but this worked really well, in my opinion, the slow built, the gradual emotional pull, the trigger and then the burst of feelings. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411606460i/11254964._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>•*´¨`*•.¸¸.•*´¨`*•.¸¸.•*´¨`*•.¸¸.•*´¨`*••*´¨`*•.¸¸.•*´¨`*•.¸<br><i>Pre-review 9/23/2014</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Deacon, my new neighbor... (A girl can dream!)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411429925i/11226588._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and ornery and stubborn Cassidy... <b>AKA</b> Bossy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253987._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253988._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cassie owns of a dream business in Colorado... Come on you know you want to go there. KA certainly gave me craving some time away in Colorado... All the Alpha males are from THERE! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253989._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253990._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She currently has a a regular visitor, you can find him in cabin <b>ELEVEN.</b><br><br><img skilled and you DON'T WANT TO MISS <s>THAT</s> <b>HIM</b>! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411600385i/11253994._SY540_.jpg" width="400"
