<div id="review_1062589099" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062589099" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062589099?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062589099" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14050656143851468948"><b>5 what are you doing to me KA? STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572707i/11813626.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There was nothing there. He was standing. His blood was coursing through his veins. He was breathing. But that was it. He existed. He did not live. He did not feel. He did not smile. He did not laugh.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Hands down my favourite Kristen Ashley book I read so far. I really feel like she stepped up her games with this one. Of course there were a few hit and miss things in the last three books, mainly pacing and story flow. But with Deacon I believe she </span>
  <span id="freeText14050656143851468948" style="display:none"><b>5 what are you doing to me KA? STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572707i/11813626.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There was nothing there. He was standing. His blood was coursing through his veins. He was breathing. But that was it. He existed. He did not live. He did not feel. He did not smile. He did not laugh.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Hands down my favourite Kristen Ashley book I read so far. I really feel like she stepped up her games with this one. Of course there were a few hit and miss things in the last three books, mainly pacing and story flow. But with Deacon I believe she hit the nail on the head...FOR ME. I can't stress this enough. KA books are beautiful for me, but they might not be for the next person. Her style is very unique and needs a little getting used to. Some love it and some hate it.<br><br>Now, this story was beautifully crafted, the characters felt very well developed, three dimensional and for me personally it was one of those swoon fests, where I sit in my reading chair, drinking my coffee -ignoring everything around me...while letting a little sigh slip every once in a while. I just felt like coming home.<br><br>The thing I liked the most is that Deacon and Cassie are the main characters here, and I mean it. There are very few side characters and even guest appearances by our former heroes, but they are all a side note. It’s very quiet out there in the mountains and beside the cabin guests there aren’t many people around.<br><br>I know what you’re thinking...shut up and tell us what it's all about, Flo! No problem here it goes:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It's a beautiful war, baby." He dipped so close, the tips of our noses brushed but his eyes never left mine. "And I...just… won.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415792195i/11846484.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cassidy Swallow</b> has had one dream all of her life. Ever since her parents took her on holiday in the Colorado Mountains the first time she imagined owning a few cabins and living her life filled with nature, breathtaking beauty and skiing.<br><br>At twenty-four she is finally living the dream. Right out of college she found some cabins for sale and with a little help from her dad she bought them and is now determined to fix them up.<br><br>Cassie is a hard working, independent and very kind woman. She knows what she wants and she is willing to sacrifice for her dreams and work hard. Her boyfriend Grant, who initially was quite fond of the whole moving to Colorado idea is not so hard working and more of a live your life on the girlfriend's dime kind of guy. <br><br>No surprise that a lot of fights and drama ensue. I think you can imagine that this relationship is doomed and dead in the water.<br><br>But there is hope...in cabin ELEVEN!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Not easy, fightin’ your pull. Wantin’ to be right here. Knowin’ I was no good for you. Prayin’ you’d get a man so when I’d come back I’d have a reason to stay away.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415792195i/11846485.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Deacon Gates</b> is the definition of mystery. For starters, we don't know his real name until halfway through the book. Mister tall, dark and brooding goes by the name <b>John Priest</b> most of the time. You guessed it, there is a story behind it and you have to read the book to find out.<br><br>Deacon he has been visiting the <i>Glacier Lily Cottages</i> and cabin eleven, since before Cassie added the new name. One day he appears for one of his frequent visits and finds not only a new owner, but also said owner in a fight with her bastard boyfriend.<br><br>There is absolutely no indication as to what he thinks about that, since the book is written in Cassie's POV and he has the brooding-and-I'm-dangerous-don't-look-at-me mask down to a T. Only clue we get is that Deacon comes back...a few times a year, not saying much, spending time in his favourite cabin #11, occasionally helping Cassie out of a bind - or turning up on Christmas.<br><br>In fact it takes six years before the relationship turns into something else.<br><br>Didn't see that one coming did you? Yeah, patience is essential here.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“In this bed, out of it. Naked or not. No boundaries. All in. Nothin’ held back.” He pressed his hips between my legs and I drew in a sharp breath. “You’re all mine, Cassidy, every fuckin’ inch. And I’m all yours, just the same.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416062266i/11883594.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is quite obvious that this book is a slow burner, but in the best of ways. Excellent execution on the author's part and addictive like nothing else. Maybe coffee...but you know that already. ;D<br><br>I love the way Cassie and Deacon slowly feel each other out. Imagine Cassie trying to pet a wild animal and she makes a slow and careful approach. It takes a long time to get there, but eventually all the walls come down...a kitchen table may or may not be involved. And what happens after is incredibly fascinating to read and makes my heart go all mushy. It’s just a gorgeous and sometimes painful love story; about partnership, healing and trust.<br><br>Deacon is such a stunning character. He is broken almost beyond repair, has one hell of a difficult past, which forced him to give up on life and happiness a long time ago. Cassie is his silver lining...he just has to accept the fact and get his moves on.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’d been right all those years ago. His eyes had the power to make you feel what he was feeling. Cold to your soul. Or warm in a way you’d never again feel a chill. And that was how I felt right then with Deacon’s eyes smiling into mine. Like I’d never feel cold again.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>By now you know I loved this book and I'm sorry for rambling like a crazy person without giving too much away, but I wanted to write a long and hopefully fitting review, to a book I shall forever be happy to re-read. ;D<br><br>Also, and that's just for my kinky ones out there...once Deacon and Cassie decide to do something about the attraction they had from day one they also play a little...and sometimes they play a lot. <br><br>Wonderful book that hit all my hot spots. From start to finish something I would recommend to anyone who will listen.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer2265664802145660586">4.5 Warm, Sweet, Fluffy Cloud Stars ❤<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/PicMonkeyCollage_zps27ba7c72.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br><br><br>I’m sure you’re not surprised that I loved this one. KA has yet to disappoint me really. A couple of her recent books have fallen just a tiny bit short for me but I’ll keep going back. <br><br>The Unfinished Heroes series is one of my favorites. Each of the hero’s had a sharp edge to them, were off the grid and of course they were badasses. But with Deacon, there was something different about him. For me this difference was his sweetness and I LOVED it.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Woman, if you don’t already know that you’ve been on my mind every day for the last six years, I got no clue how to communicate that to you. Now that I’ve had you, that shit has not changed. It’s just got worse. Now it’s not every day. It’s every hour. I don’t fight it, every minute. Fuck, every second, I don’t keep it in check. Every second, I’m thinkin’ of you, thinkin’ of gettin’ shit done, but only so I can get back to you.” ~ Deacon</i>
</b><br><br>Cassidy Swallow is following her dream. It is a simple one. She has left home with her boyfriend Grant to live in the Colorado Mountains, renting beautiful cabins while living in all this beauty herself. She knows being a business owner is not an easy life but she is willing to work hard to make her dream come true.<br><br>Cassidy and Grant feel the pressures of the hard work involved in making this all work. Cassidy is willing to do whatever it takes but for Grant things begin to unravel. Grant is no longer that person she fell in love with, the one that made the promises of living out her dream. <br><br>When Cassidy first meets John Priest (Deacon) he is masked, cold and detached. But she cannot deny this sense of a connection with him. She is drawn to him in a way she can’t explain. As John Priest drifts in and out of Cassidy’s life over a number of years there was an ache, a slow burn between them that neither would acknowledge until one night. Everything changes.<br><br><b>Deacon ~</b><br><br>I said at the beginning that Deacon’s difference is his sweetness. But that is just a sliver of him that I grabbed hold of. Deacon just existed. He didn’t feel things. He didn’t want to. The last time he did, his life had fallen apart. He slipped away from everything and everyone who had been important to him to live a life that didn’t have much meaning.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/deacon_zpsea3cd003.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412432298i/11374799.jpg" alt=" photo deacon_zpsea3cd003.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>“Where do you wanna be when you’re eighty?” “Don’t fuck up and blow my shot, sittin’ on my ass on a chair that I’m glad now has a pad, next to a decent woman with beautiful eyes, lips made to be kissed, and phenomenal hair, listenin’ to a river and starin’ at some trees.”</i><br><br><b>Cassidy ~</b><br><br>She lived her life with a sense of determination that made her beautiful inside and out. Cassidy spoke her mind, would not settle and was fiery as all hell.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/cassidy_zpse159e6af.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412432299i/11374800._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo cassidy_zpse159e6af.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>“I’d been right all those years ago. His eyes had the power to make you feel what he was feeling. Cold to your soul. Or warm in a way you’d never again feel a chill. And that was how I felt right then with Deacon’s eyes smiling into mine. Like I’d never feel cold again.”</i><br><br>I have to admit, things were just chugging along and I was hoping it was going to pick up a bit. Then I felt it. I knew things were going to change and they sure as hell did.<br><br>KA did not disappoint when it came to the sex scenes. Has she ever? Deacon and Cassie were explosive and when they began to “play”, HOLY SHIT things were HOT. Deacon loved hard and Cassie harder. She gave her body to Deacon freely and Deacon worshiped <b>EVERY</b> single <b>INCH</b> of <b>HER</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/deaconcollage_zps5e187a3b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412432299i/11374801.jpg" alt=" photo deaconcollage_zps5e187a3b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Watching things shift within Deacon was something else. This badass was surrendering to Cassidy’s genuine love she had for him and it pained him. I just found that to be beautiful. And with each piece of him that he was handing over, Cassidy was holding on tight. <br><br>But there was a part of himself that he couldn’t let go of. He couldn’t give her everything and for Cassidy that just wasn’t good enough. How does that saying go? If you love something set it free. If it comes back it’s yours, if it doesn’t it wasn’t meant to be. She needed to let Deacon go.<br><br>Such an amazing read. KA doesn’t miss a beat. She gives us everything from freakin amazing characters, detail after detail on the beauty of the location, scorching sex and she always gives us that little something extra . Don’t let this one pass you by ladies!! Deacon is a must read.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/final_zps3a3bf516.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412432299i/11374802._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo final_zps3a3bf516.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2265664802145660586" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1362535804" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1362535804" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1362535804?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22846841-deacon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen">kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1362535804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13706062208998246044"><b> 3.5 Beautiful war stars </b><br/><br/>This is when I really wish Goodreads had half stars. Because this book really is a strong 3.5 and not a 4 for me. But I wouldn't lower it to a 3. So I'll make do. <br/><br/><b> <i> “Badasses know what they want, definitely know what they need, and don’t settle for anything less.” </i> </b><br/><br/>At the age of twenty four Cassidy took out a loan and bought a small smattering of 11 run down cabins in the Colorado Mountains. This story takes place over the next 6-8 years and while Cassidy is slowly fixin</span>
  <span id="freeText13706062208998246044" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 Beautiful war stars </b><br><br>This is when I really wish Goodreads had half stars. Because this book really is a strong 3.5 and not a 4 for me. But I wouldn't lower it to a 3. So I'll make do. <br><br><b> <i> “Badasses know what they want, definitely know what they need, and don’t settle for anything less.” </i> </b><br><br>At the age of twenty four Cassidy took out a loan and bought a small smattering of 11 run down cabins in the Colorado Mountains. This story takes place over the next 6-8 years and while Cassidy is slowly fixing up the place, she has one returning customer, and that's the brooding and mysterious John Priest. He's gruff, doesn't speak much, and a little bit rude. But there's a draw between John and Cassidy, and over the years as he keeps coming back to Glacier Lily (the name of the cabins), the two begin to give in.<br><br>Cassidy knew from the first moment she saw him he was dead inside, she just didn't know how far gone he really was. Can Cassidy save him from himself? Or will he break her in the process?<br><br><b> <i> “Woman, if you don’t already know that you’ve been on my mind every day for the last six years, I got no clue how to communicate that to you. Now that I’ve had you, that shit has not changed. It’s just got worse.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I enjoyed this book I really did, but being The Queen of romance that Kristen Ashley is, this series is not my favorite by her. Yes, it's a little darker and has a lot more kinky sex, but her usual depth was missing for me with this one. Maybe because the plot was so centralized around these two characters? All in all this book is a great example of same formula and different character names with more kinky sex. <br><br>Plus, those of you who know me well know my golden rule: <b> You fuck up, then you'd better fucking grovel. </b> And I'm sorry but in my honest opinion, Deacon was forgiven for his actions WAY too easily. I understand how messed up he was and why, and he did his best to mend fences, but I lose all respect for the main female characters when they just give in and take a dude back. To me it makes them a little bit more of a doormat.<br><br><b> <i> “You’re a vulnerability,” he ground out. “My vulnerability. I have no vulnerabilities. I spent years shavin’ every last one away from me so there was nothin’ left. Now I got one, a big one, and I do not give one fuck.” </i> </b><br><br>Not to go on about what I didn't like so here are some positives: I love stories about messed up men. Cassidy didn't fix Deacon all by herself but she led him on the path back to a good life and back to being the good man he once was. Cassidy worked her ass off to succeed and she earned every little bit of success that came her way. I find that admirable. We as readers got to see her grow over the years, she just wasn't magically successful like some women in romance novels who pop out of college a ruthless business woman making millions. So nice to read about a hardworking woman. <br><br>So overall, I think KA fans who loved Knight would love this one. Being as Knight wasn't my cup of tea, I wasn't in love with this book either. But honestly, (in a not so eloquent phrasing) Kristen Ashley books are like chocolate, even if it's not the best or the most gourmet, it's still enjoyable and fun to consume.<br><br><b> <i> “It's a beautiful war, baby." He dipped so close, the tips of our noses brushed but his eyes never left mine. "And I...just… won.” </i> </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13706062208998246044" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10102073645473244342"><i>5+ make me happy stars</i><br/><blockquote>

  <b>
    <i>“Best lay, bar none. Funniest bitch, bar none. Finest woman, bar none. And all of that better every day.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421027937i/13312074._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At thirteen, Cassidy dreamed up a plan to own peaceful cabins up by the river in the Colorado mountain, sitting on her porch and enjoying the peace that this place brings. Now years later she is finally ready to live that dream; she isn't scared or put off by all of the work that needs to be done, but it would be nice to not have to go at it alone. John Priest stumbled on this dream, and over the course of the years he's made it a sad excuse for a home. Never giving anything away, just content to be in the cabin in remote location fighting a strong pull for the beautiful owner. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Not easy, fightin’ your pull. Wantin’ to be right here. Knowin’ I was no good for you. Prayin’ you’d get a man so when I’d come back I’d have a reason to stay away.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He's tried all he can to stay away, not knowing when he would come, or what he would do, trying to find a reason to let her live her life without him in it. Cassidy knowns nothing about the stranger in Cabin Eleven, but from the very first day they met, she can't help but hope that this man she should fear, would sit and talk a while and possibly do a whole lot more...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Why cabin eleven was home to me for a few days every year, the only home I had, ’cause you were there.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Deep in her bones she knows, just as Deacon knows, that what this is, this burn they'd shared for years, is nothing to turn your back on. Risking the change to find what it all means, demands a whole lot of trust. Deacon doesn't share, she knows it's for the best, but how can she give her all to a man she doesn't know in the most basic sense. She knows the man he is inside but is that enough? For now it has to be...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The one. The world. The man made for me. The man I was going to fall in love with. The only man I’d ever really love. That was why I’d made my choice. That was why I would long for him if he’d decided to leave me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> Struggling with wanting to be happy, and wanting it all, Cassie has to decide if being with a man like Deacon is worth the lies and the heartache every time he goes away, hoping that one day he would stay and never leave...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love is trust, Cassie, you taught me that.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421027937i/13312075.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Deacon</b> was everything I hoped it would be and so much more... A alpha man that only KA can create, how he can be so strong, protective and controlling but do it with such tenderness. He earned his Hero title with all that he's been through and Cassie was the perfect woman for him to get him to come back to the world of the living. Cassie is an old soul, who never wanted much just a man to love her and to grow old with sitting on her porch and watching the peace of the river flow by. She is stubborn and is a total boss, no pushover here at all. Deacon was a man who drowned in his past but in Cassie found the breath brought back in him, making him smile, laugh and simply happy. <br><br>Their story was told from both their POV, which is a real treat, getting to see their turmoil, their happiness and their longing. Everything about them screamed too good to be true, always waiting for the last shoe to drop and when it did, holy hell, did it ever. A wonderful heartfelt tale of a man who lost his way and the woman who guided him back. It was HOT, smart, witty, funny and beautiful; just what anyone would expect from the great Kristen Ashley! <br><br><i>***The ending, holy shit, I am super excited for who's book is up next, because that bad boy has a lot to make right...and I have a feeling the entire gang will be back, full force!<br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10102073645473244342" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer715337885" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10970690786817023161">4--<b>Woman</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/>I'll admit, I don't read a lot of KA books! Frankly, they're just too damn long! This series is the only one I've been consistent with and it still felt like it took me forever to read this one!<br/><br/>But with that being said, every KA book I do end up reading I end up liking. It's just a matter of taking the plunge! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411929796ra/11301292.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So....I don't have a lot to compare to, but I enjoyed this one! Even though honestly not much happened! <br/><br/>It's always been Cassidy's dream to live in the mountains if Colora</span>
  <span id="freeText10970690786817023161" style="display:none">4--<b>Woman</b>--Stars!!<br><br>I'll admit, I don't read a lot of KA books! Frankly, they're just too damn long! This series is the only one I've been consistent with and it still felt like it took me forever to read this one!<br><br>But with that being said, every KA book I do end up reading I end up liking. It's just a matter of taking the plunge! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411929796ra/11301292.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So....I don't have a lot to compare to, but I enjoyed this one! Even though honestly not much happened! <br><br>It's always been Cassidy's dream to live in the mountains if Colorado! In her early 20s, she buys a set of run down cabins and sets about making her dreams a reality! <br><br>Over the next six years, Deacon rents cabin 11. Deacon is a typical KA alpha male! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411929355ra/11301208.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Most of the book Deacon remains a mystery. He pops in and out of Cassidy's life. They rarely speak but there's that underlying connection that burns between them! <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“In this bed, out of it. Naked or not. No boundaries. All in. Nothin’ held back.” He pressed his hips between my legs and I drew in a sharp breath. “You’re all mine, Cassidy, every fuckin’ inch. And I’m all yours, just the same.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>You know from the other books in the series, that Deacon is involved in some unsavory activities. He can't and won't open up to Cassidy. But she's willing to take whatever Deacon will give her. <br><br>Deacon's resolve finally crumbles and he gives in to what he feels for Cassidy! He still leaves for periods of time to work but he always returns back to Cassidy! The more time they are together, the more Deacon wants to leave that life behind. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403826351ra/10150322.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Deacon's past becomes part of his present, Cassidy has to decide if the bits and pieces Deacon has given her are enough. And Deacon will have to let go of his past once and for all if he wants a future with Cassidy! <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“It's a beautiful war, baby." He dipped so close, the tips of our noses brushed but his eyes never left mine. "And I...just… won.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>While the majority of the plot focused on Deacon and Cassidy and the development of their relationship, I was really never bored! Deacon was just as drool worthy as every other KA alpha hero I've read about. He was fierce, he was protective and he loved Cassidy hard! Cassidy was a strong heroine. She was sarcastic, she was stubborn, and she didn't let Deacon get away with anything! <br><br>The kink was a bit weird for me, but there wasn't an over abundance of it. The vanilla sex was off the charts hot though! <br><br>So yeah, I liked this one. I liked Deacon, I liked Cassidy and I especially liked Bossy and Priest!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411929355i/11301209.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_733972261" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733972261" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733972261?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=sept2014">sept2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733972261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2450525595053909298"><b>Full review now posted</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b>Deacon<br/><b>Series:</b>Unfinished Hero #4<br/><b>Author:</b>Kristen Ashley<br/><b>Release date:</b>September 23, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b>3.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201528.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409782389i/11021373.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well. Here I go again, rating another Kristen Ashley book...average?? Kristen Ashley is so much more than average. She's put out many of my all-time favorite books. So amazing that I'm stuck to those pages so hard you couldn't tear me away if my house was on fire. I would still be clutching my book saying in annoyanc</span>
  <span id="freeText2450525595053909298" style="display:none"><b>Full review now posted</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b>Deacon<br><b>Series:</b>Unfinished Hero #4<br><b>Author:</b>Kristen Ashley<br><b>Release date:</b>September 23, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b>3.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201528.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409782389i/11021373.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well. Here I go again, rating another Kristen Ashley book...average?? Kristen Ashley is so much more than average. She's put out many of my all-time favorite books. So amazing that I'm stuck to those pages so hard you couldn't tear me away if my house was on fire. I would still be clutching my book saying in annoyance, "Hey! I'm reading here!" I've re-read some of her books so many times, I could probably recite long stretches of dialogue without pausing to think. This author has the ability to transport me into her character's minds, emotions, and lives and make me want to stay there for a good, long time. That being said, I feel like crying, but this book in the end, wasn't a spectacular read for me. I need a hug, guys.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411654226ra/11261495.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It started out so fresh, promising, and SO exciting. I was absolutely positive this was going to be a 5 star read. And then something happened. The interaction between the hero and heroine started feeling less thrilling and more repetitive. It started to feel like I was dragging instead of racing. And the sex went from "Holy Mother-that's hot" to "What?!" And I was left wondering, what went wrong?<br><br>I'm breaking this book into two halves because I had a polar opposite reaction to both parts.<br><br><b>First half:</b><br><br>It started out with a bang. Kristen Ashley tends to stick with what she does best: Alpha heroes, sassy heroines, and lots of bantering and antics. Which is just fine because she does that to perfection. But this time around, there was a refreshing, distinctive feel to the story. It was just so <i>different</i>. And I was loving it. <br><br>Cassie bought some beautiful cabins in the mountains for a song with plans to fix them up and experience her simple dream of living in that beautiful peace of country and having a peaceful fulfilling life. Deacon is the mysterious, intense, and silent man that rents the same cabin from her off and on throughout the months and years. Her first impression of him was that he was intimidating and sexy in a really scary way. His look burned right through her-I felt the heat between them immediately.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409782389i/11021374._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved how they just had brief moments of interactions through a long period of time. They gradually fell deeper without having to say a word. The push and pull between them was perfection. <br><br><b>There would always be thoughts in the back of my mind plaguing me, haunting me, making me wonder, if he let me in, even just a little, how it could have been.</b><br><br>The anticipation that was built was a thick and tangible thing. It was crazy good! The moment Deacon's willpower to stay away finally crashed and burned, I was eating it up. It was delicious, sexy, and fierce. <br><br>When they finally get together, it's finally revealed what was behind his stoic, impenetrable wall. He never gave a hint of what he was feeling away out of protection for her, but now he can't hold himself back anymore. Just a taste of her has him addicted. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409782389i/11021375._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Not easy, fighting' your pull. Wantin' to be right here. Knowin' I was no good for you. Prayin' you'd get a man so when I'd come back I'd have a reason to stay away."</b><br><br>They tentatively try to forge a relationship together. They both realize that this thing they have is special. Despite Deacon's inability to share about much of anything about himself and his need to leave for periods of time unexpectedly without warning for work...Cassie is blindly putting her trust in him and taking a leap of faith. When Deacon is with her, he's everything she's always wanted in a man-intensely passionate, supportive, and he seems to savor the peace that she's found on that side of the mountain just as much as her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409782389i/11021376._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Second half:</b><br><br>This is pretty much where it got stuck for me. My genuine feelings were that everything I was enjoying before started getting stuck on repeat and I started to feel that the plot was slowing way down as the erotica was building in the sex.<br><br><u>The kink:</u><br>I already knew that this book was going to be kinky. I mean, it's her erotic series so I was already expecting it. But for me, the kink wasn't working. I wasn't feeling it, it honestly felt weird. You're warned in the beginning about the anal play, I knew it was there, and I was fine with it. I read erotic books so that's a non issue. But what I didn't care for was the scene with him trying to prove his total trust in her during sex at the end. I couldn't conceive of him ever being okay with letting her do that to him-he even told her earlier in the book that he didn't care for it and yet suddenly he was asking her to do it and then...enjoying it? It felt off and it felt like it was added purely for the sake of pushing the erotic boundaries. Maybe it's just me. Plus, Cassie's secret desires that were revealed didn't feel natural to the rest of the story. They kind of came out of nowhere and vanilla disappeared with a POOF.<br><br><u>Second thing I wasn't feeling:</u>The serious repetition of them discussing how much of a badass he is. (There are 52 badass references in the book. 52.) At first, I thought it was cute and funny, but after a while, it was seriously excessive. The more they talked about it, the less badass he seemed. Do badasses actually refer to <i>themselves</i> as badass? Maybe if we were shown why he is one a few times, it would work better, but after they hook up the story pretty much centers around them building their relationship. <br><br><u>Lastly:</u>It bothered me how naive and trusting she was of him after a while. She blindly believed his integrity based on....what? He was so secretive with her! And after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he leaves her without fighting for her, rather than open up about his past and explain himself, she takes him back without much resistance. AT ALL. She made it way too easy on him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I wish I could have rated this higher given the fact that I insanely loved the first half, but I didn't end the book with a happy feeling. I felt conflicted and out of sorts. I loved the dynamic between Cassie and Deacon. I loved that there was a fresh originality to the plot that was so exciting to read. I loved this couple's passion and intensity. But as much as I loved those things, I didn't feel them all the way through. Kristen Ashley is cemented as one of my favorite authors however, and I know so many people won't agree with all my issues, so if you're planning on reading this, It could very easily be a huge hit for you. This has the potential to be a huge success.<br><br><i>**ARC provided in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Facebook" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768485i/8452963.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/25650476-deacon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1296946414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14927773551672640601"><i>Written June 6, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>4.2 Happy Smiling Stars - Sweet story, great narrator and just the right length</b><br/><br/>The new KA audiobook published in April 2015. Only $6 for 11:20 hrs well written romance narrated by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7205549.Stella_Bloom' title='Stella Bloom' rel='nofollow noopener'>Stella Bloom</a>. <br/><br/><i>~ My twentieth book by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a>.... in two years. ~ </i><br/><br/><a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>A man who thought he lost everything</b> found the woman who gave him everything. Yet another happiness pills from a contemporary romances master. Everything is here, just to soak up and enjoy.<br/><br/>********************</span>
  <span id="freeText14927773551672640601" style="display:none"><i>Written June 6, 2015</i><br><br><b>4.2 Happy Smiling Stars - Sweet story, great narrator and just the right length</b><br><br>The new KA audiobook published in April 2015. Only $6 for 11:20 hrs well written romance narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7205549.Stella_Bloom" title="Stella Bloom" rel="nofollow noopener">Stella Bloom</a>. <br><br><i>~ My twentieth book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a>.... in two years. ~ </i><br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>A man who thought he lost everything</b> found the woman who gave him everything. Yet another happiness pills from a contemporary romances master. Everything is here, just to soak up and enjoy.<br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><i>Colorado Mountains</i><br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/City%20and%20nature%20etc/winter/image.jpg4_zpsip3fly0q.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438208i/15096774.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg4_zpsip3fly0q.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“Badasses know what they want, definitely know what they need, and don’t settle for anything less.” <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438515i/15096807.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘The one. The world. The man made for me. The man I was going to fall in love with. The only man I’d ever really love.’</blockquote><br><i>Deacon</i> is the story about <b>Cassidy "Cassie" Swallow</b> who wants to fulfill her childhood dreams about the mountain (winter) land. Living a sweet life, skiing, owning some nice cabins and living in a house by a river surrounded by aspen and pine. She is still young and she has it. <br><br>One of Cassie's first guest tenants is the mysterious <b>John Priest (aka Deacon Gates)</b>. He is soon a "steady" guest, comes a few times every years, stay a couple of days or a week, they don't talk that much but Cassie can't forget him. Cabin 11 is his, decorated for him. This big (dangerous? — but tempting) stranger becomes more interesting, awaited and important in Cassie's life. <br><br>Than one day something happens and Deacon stay. A grand steaming hot love story starts at last...<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/image.jpg2_zps0w0drapk.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438352i/15096792.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg2_zps0w0drapk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br>*********************************************************<br><br><i>Deacon</i> has it all (...more or less). Some freaking sweeeeet tender moments, hot steaming bedrooms adventures, friends and family stuff, food and cake baking, heartbreaking scenes, grand lovely "speaks", a tough manly grunting KA-man and a super über nice talkative KA-woman. We get the usual as interior details, girls talk, guys talk, dirty talking, slightly strange words to give affection to the woman you love (this time 'Woman'), and a extremely sensitive but strong sexy alpha male (three-words) hero. <br><br><b>All in all another yummy sweet and heartwarming cozy</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> tale. This time in the more (kinky) explicit erotic romances genre (as this "Unfinished Hero" series is expected to be). <br><br>There are parts with BDSM like kink, toys and playing. Not my favorite topic in romances but Ms Ashley tells it in a beautiful tender way. It never went to far —for me— it just felt like love making and ended as a romantic way of showing deep trust. For them both. I liked that. Jippie, for equality ...everywhere! <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438515i/15096807.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Then he settled us in our customary going to sleep position. I listened to his breath even and I was relaxed, totally. Happy, completely. Fulfilled, undeniably. <br>But I still could talk. <br>“I loved that.” <br>“Got that when you came hard and loud, nearly bowing the headboard.” <br>I grinned against his chest.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts/image.jpg1_zpsyznlofa2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438902i/15096848.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpsyznlofa2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>Sometimes it becomes slightly tedious with this grunting cave-man talk, and very strange monosyllabic communication, but whatever, you can not but be charmed and enamored. ~ As always. Simply awesome.<br><br>*********************************************************<br><br>This <i>Deacon</i> novel is #4 in the (standalones) "Unfinished Hero" series. My third read. ~ I liked the very kinky #1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510231115?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight (4 stars)</a> and liked even more (loved) the easier and nicer #3 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537554159?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Raid (4.2 stars)</a>. <br><br>The narrator <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7205549.Stella_Bloom" title="Stella Bloom" rel="nofollow noopener">Stella Bloom</a> here does it great. She is perfect for a Kristen Ashley story on audio. Looking forward to hear her lovely voice again. (She is very good doing male characters too.) ~ Applause!! <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> As a VERY nice gift we get to meet the whole "series"-gang also. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ — <i>Daisy &amp; Marcus Sloan</i> (from the 'Rock Chicks' series) — <i>Anya &amp; Knight Sebring</i> and their girls <i>Kat and Kasha</i> (#1) — <i>Tucker &amp; Sylvie Creed</i> and their baby <i>Jesse</i> (#2) — and (Deacon's best friend) <i>Raid &amp; Hanna Miller</i> (#3). —  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Just short but it was fun.<br><br><b>I LIKE - swoon-worthy men and sweet grand love</b><br><br><br>******<br>Deacon's song to Cassie: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438515i/15096807.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘I listened again. <br>On the third go, I went to Google and looked up “Beautiful War” lyrics. It was by <i>Kings of Leon</i>. <br>I read them. <br>Then I listened again.’<br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=2" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417196564ra/12258903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/RVDc6bYy3j4">http://youtu.be/RVDc6bYy3j4</a><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433438515i/15096807.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg18_zpsig2qkeyv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1029497741" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1029497741" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1029497741?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1029497741" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8470927156552034031"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411650102i/11261030.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What makes Kristen Ashley’s books unputdownable? The fantastic storyline? The handsome, sexy alpha males? The smart, sassy heroines? The unique style? Or maybe the brilliant writing? Well,…all of the above, because nothing compares with KA’s books, at least for me. Every single book that I read by Kristen Ashley moved me in some way, every single book left me reflecting, every book warmed my heart.<br/><br/>I must admit, this book wasn’t my favorite by this author, (because for me, no book is mor</span>
  <span id="freeText8470927156552034031" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411650102i/11261030.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What makes Kristen Ashley’s books unputdownable? The fantastic storyline? The handsome, sexy alpha males? The smart, sassy heroines? The unique style? Or maybe the brilliant writing? Well,…all of the above, because nothing compares with KA’s books, at least for me. Every single book that I read by Kristen Ashley moved me in some way, every single book left me reflecting, every book warmed my heart.<br><br>I must admit, this book wasn’t my favorite by this author, (because for me, no book is more wonderful than “At Peace” ), but it was for sure a wonderful experience.<br> <br><i>"Deacon”</i> is book four in Kristen Ashley’s <i>“Unfinished Hero”</i> series. This is the story of a broken man, Deacon and the wonderful woman who will heal his heart, his soul and give him what he needs and more, Cassidy (Cassie).<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It's a beautiful war, baby." <br>He dipped so close, the tips of our noses <br>brushed but his eyes never left mine. <br>"And I...just won."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I’m not gonna retell the blurb, because I don’t want to give anything away..so..<br><br>I loved both Deacon and Cassie. Like any Kristen Ashley’s characters, they are strong characters and they are very well developed through the entire story. Cassie is your usual KA’s heroine. She’s smart, she’s strong, she’s sassy, she knows what she wants and she loves, with all her heart. <br><br>Deacon is dark and he has, let’s just say, an unusual job. He can’t escape the past and the memories are still haunting him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He was breathing.<br> But that was it.<br> He existed.<br> He did not live. He did not feel. He did not smile. He did not laugh.”<br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really, really felt for him.<br><br>Cassie will change him and will affect him like no other. With Cassie he will feel alive, he will want to live, he will want a future, he will want to love again. Deacon is bossy, protective and most of all he loves Cassie. And when a KA’s alpha male loves, he loves…till the end. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Anything. You want it, I got it in me to give it to you, you got anything from me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411654189i/11261479.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story presents Deacon and Cassie relationship, the good and the bad, how they learn to live and love again. I loved all the beautiful and sweet moments between them. There are plenty of them and each one of them left me with a smile on my face. I loved how they get to know each other, trust each other and how open they are with each other. <br><br>The sex scenes are extremely hot, intense, passionate, sometimes vanilla and sometimes kinky... <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Baby, that pussy on my mouth, your ass in my hands, the noises you make fillin’ the room, knowin’ I get to drive deep in your wet, tight cunt while you’re still moanin’ for me. Then after I give it to you, and you give it to me, I get to bed down with you tucked tight. You don’t think that makes me happy, you’re fuckin’ crazy.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>...and their chemistry is so great.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411654252i/11261496.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The banter between Deacon and Cassie is fantastic and the funny moments hilarious.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Fuckin’ beautiful, but a pain in my goddamned ass,” he muttered.<br> “Same here, Supreme Leader of the Badasses.”<br> “Case in point.”<br> “You’re messing up my hair.”<br> “Another case in point.”<br> “Are you gonna kiss me or just stand there, messing up my hair and annoying me?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Loved the beautiful epilogue - all the lovely moments between Deacon and Cassie, between them and their friends, between them and their families. The story and the characters like in every book by this author felt real and their story relatable. <br><br>I expected more action, but the lack of it and the lack of drama didn’t bother me too much, maybe because I enjoyed so much the love story between Deacon and Cassie. <br><br>All in all, <i>“Deacon”</i> was a great story with an engaging storyline, endearing characters and like always captivating writing.<br><br>Can't recommend this one highly enough!!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love is trust, Cassie, you taught me that.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8470927156552034031" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer10111561797700790647"><b>3.25 to 3.5 Stars but I'm rounding up<b><br/><br/>I truly liked but didn't love this one. I've been disappointed in the post-douchebag reactions my KA heroines have been exhibiting as of late and I'm happy to say Cassie kinda, sorta in her own way stood firm. I also loved the fact Deacon never blamed Cassidy for his actions because his baggage was all on him. I think my overall mehness with this one comes from the fact that every KA book is indeed heavily laced with KAisms. I'm making that a word, by the way</b></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10111561797700790647" style="display:none"><b>3.25 to 3.5 Stars but I'm rounding up<b><br /><br />I truly liked but didn't love this one. I've been disappointed in the post-douchebag reactions my KA heroines have been exhibiting as of late and I'm happy to say Cassie kinda, sorta in her own way stood firm. I also loved the fact Deacon never blamed Cassidy for his actions because his baggage was all on him. I think my overall mehness with this one comes from the fact that every KA book is indeed heavily laced with KAisms. I'm making that a word, by the way. Lots of "yeah" used as a question, whispered answers and men going deep.<br /><br />My favorite part of this book, despite the KA cliches, was Deacon' s love of Cassidy and his backstory. My heart broke just a wee bit for this man and I loved how he gathered his shit and made his life work.<br /><br />Yep, I liked it but I still miss the Kristen Ashley stories I first came to love several years ago. I need a brand spanking new Tate in the worst possible way!</b></b></span>

  <span id="freeText15963413246370873850" style="display:none">It's a sad day when you realize that KA's book just isn't doing it for you. . . <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411757292ra/11270124.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411757292ra/11270125.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411757292ra/11270126.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411757292ra/11270127.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Unpopular Opinion</u><br><br>KA lovers . . . I'm sorry. *ducks away from rotten tomatoes* <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411761926ra/11270385.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>I <b>really</b> wanted to like this one. Really. I even tried to ignore the things that I didn't like because, you know, love is blind . . . and I f*cking love Kristen Ashley's books. But it just wasn't working for me. <br><br>Why?<br><br>• I felt like the characters were unoriginal. I feel like I'm reading about the same female MC I did in all her other books. And this wasn't a problem for me at first because I liked them. But there's only so many times I can read a different KA story with a similar female MC. They all pretty much think <b>the same thing,</b> and say <b>the same thing,</b> and act <b>the same way.</b> There were very few moments where I felt Cassidy was different. And I cried whenever those hints went away.<br><br>• <b>The constant repetion</b>. For inflection? Emphasis? No. Just no. <br><blockquote>
<i>On his knees on the floor, his mouth between my legs.<br>Feeding.<br>God. <br>Oh God. <br>Not feeding.<br><b>Feeding.</b></i><br><br>***<br><br><i>Okay, apparently Milagros hand't read my mood, <b>she'd read my mood</b>.<i><br><br>***<br><br><i>Then I heard her say, "You sound good."<br>I grinned as I successfully settled the casserole dish on the rack in the oven. "I am good."<br>There was silence for [a] moment before she said "No, Cassie, <b>you sound good."</b></i></i></i>
</blockquote><br>One or two times, okay. But this was too much.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411758416ra/11270182.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And it doesn't only happen in this book. <br><br>• I was waiting for things to turn around. It's Kristen Ashley, if anybody can change my opinion . . . it's her.<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411759146ra/11270251.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>But even the storyline left me a little . . . <i>meh.</i> There was no action, nothing to really keep me going except Deacon's past. And not even <i>I</i> am such a heartless bitch that his past didn't pull on my heartstrings. But I wasn't <b>
  <i>connected</i>
</b> to the story . . . so even though I did hurt for him, I didn't feel as much as I could have. <br><br>• Word count for Badass: 52<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411763697ra/11270465.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>What saved this book a little, for me, was the first 15 percent, the last 20 percent, and the sex scenes. That's about it. <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411765160ra/11270587.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><b>Rating: 2.5 stars</b></span>

<div id="review_1062680719" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062680719" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062680719?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/25650476-deacon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kinky">kinky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2014">favourites-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062680719" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13176008534313704476"><b>I'm glad I followed the impulse...</b><br/><br/>It's like that feeling you get when you stand in front of your full wardrobe and complain of nothing to wear. I have heaps of books to read, an Audible membership that gives me discounts, even a credit to satisfy an impulse. So, what do I pick? A good old KA of course. <br/><br/>It's been yonky donks since I read or listened to <i>Deacon</i>. To be honest, I think this was my first listen, but I can't say that for certain because I have a shocking memory. I'm so glad I gave into</span>
  <span id="freeText13176008534313704476" style="display:none"><b>I'm glad I followed the impulse...</b><br /><br />It's like that feeling you get when you stand in front of your full wardrobe and complain of nothing to wear. I have heaps of books to read, an Audible membership that gives me discounts, even a credit to satisfy an impulse. So, what do I pick? A good old KA of course. <br /><br />It's been yonky donks since I read or listened to <i>Deacon</i>. To be honest, I think this was my first listen, but I can't say that for certain because I have a shocking memory. I'm so glad I gave into the impulse though. I forgot how much I loved this one. <br /><br />Unlike the other Unfinished Heroes, I felt like Deacon was the most...hero...ish?!?! I don't mean donning a cape and acting all heroic (which I'm sure he's quite capable of). I mean that he is the kind of book hero that I'd happily nominate for book hero of the year. Don't get me wrong, he's far from perfect and leaves Cassie for too long "protecting her from him", but, Oh, the words he says...<br /><br />This man he has some MOVES!! This man has some WORDS!! Both his moves and his words are SEXY AND HOT!! There are some kinky scenes which I enjoyed but I admit to being surprised where KA went. Well, surprised the first time I read it. This time, and considering the <i>Honey</i> series, I guess not so surprising and more a confirmation that KA's a little kinky. 😉 <br /><br />Deacon is also sweet, caring, possessive and bossy. Sure, he was a twit for a bit, but I forgave him...and he brings cute puppies.<br /><br />Loved my re-read/listen and now it will be hard to pick anything other than another KA audio. But, which one??? Heaven and Hell or maybe Play it Safe? Decisions...decisions...<br /><br /><br />**********<br /><br /><strong>Loved it</strong><br /><br />WoW THAT WAS HOT!!!!<br /><br />That was by far the hottest book that Kristen Ashley has written. Loved the storyline and the characters, loved the epilogue and loved what this book made me feel.<br /><br />Not sure how I feel about her skimming over Raid and Hanna's conclusion to the dramas, but I'm getting the impression we'll get all the answers in Nick's story.<br /><br />Loved how the backstory was told and that Cassidy wasn't willing to put up with Deacons crap.<br /><br />Really enjoyed all of this one and loved that we got to catch up with Daisy. Kristen Ashley thank you for the experience.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13176008534313704476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
